If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\\n50: //\\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\\n54: \\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\\n55: \\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\\n56: \\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\\n57: \\n58: \\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\\n81: \\t// will requeue.\\n82: \\t//\\n83: \\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\\n84: \\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\\n85: \\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\\n86: \\t//\\n87: \\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\\n88: \\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\\n89: \\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\\n90: \\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\\n91: \\n92: \\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\\n93: \\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\\n94: \\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\\n95: \\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\\n96: \\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\\n97: }\\n98: \\n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. \t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/metrics\"\n30: \t\"github.com/cilium/cilium/pkg/promise\"\n31: )\n32: \n33: // Resource provides access to a Kubernetes resource through either\n34: // a stream of events or a read-only store.\n35: //\n36: // Observing of the events can be done from a constructor as subscriber\n37: // registration is non-blocking.\n38: //\n39: // Store() however should only be called from a start hook, or from a\n40: // goroutine forked from the start hook as it blocks until the store\n41: // has been synchronized.\n42: //\n43: // The subscriber can process the events from Events() asynchronously and in\n44: // parallel, but for each event the Done() function must be called to mark\n45: // the event as handled. If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\n50: //\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\n54: \t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\n55: \t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\n56: \tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\n57: \n58: \t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\n59: \t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\n60: \t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\n61: \t//\n62: \t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\n63: \t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\n64: \t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\n65: \t//\n66: \t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\n67: \t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\n68: \t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\n69: \t// updates:\n70: \t//\n71: \t//\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\n72: \t//\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\n73: \t//\n74: \t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\n75: \t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\n76: \t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\n77: \t// sent to the observer.\n78: \t//\n79: \t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\n80: \t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\n81: \t// will requeue.\n82: \t//\n83: \t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\n84: \t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\n85: \t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\n86: \t//\n87: \t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\n88: \t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\n89: \t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\n90: \tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\n91: \n92: \t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\n93: \t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\n94: \t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\n95: \t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\n96: \tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\n97: }\n98: \n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. Use with hive.Provide:\n100: //\n101: //\tvar exampleCell = hive.Module(\n102: //\t\t\"example\",\n103: //\t \tcell.Provide(\n104: //\t\t \t// Provide `Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]` to the hive:\n105: //\t\t \tfunc(lc cell.Lifecycle, c k8sClient.Clientset) resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod] {\n106: //\t\t\t\tlw := utils.ListerWatcherFromTyped[*slim_corev1.PodList](\n107: //\t\t\t\t\tc.Slim().CoreV1().Pods(\"\"),\n108: //\t\t\t\t)\n109: //\t\t \t\treturn resource.New(lc, lw)\n110: //\t\t \t}\n111: //\t\t}),\n112: //\t\t...\n113: //\t)\n114: //\n115: //\tfunc usePods(pods resource.Resource[*slim_corev1.Pod]) {\n116: //\t\tgo func() {\n117: //\t\t\tfor ev := range podEvents {\n118: //\t\t   \t\tonPodEvent(ev)\n119: //\t\t   \t}\n120: //\t\t}\n121: //\t\treturn e\n122: //\t}\n123: //\tfunc onPodEvent(event resource.Event[*slim_core.Pod]) {\n124: //\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n125: //\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n126: //\t\t\t// Pods have now been synced and the set of Upsert events\n127: //\t\t\t// received thus far forms a coherent snapshot.\n128: //\n129: //\t\t\t// Must always call event.Done(error) to mark the event as processed.\n130:
